Gardner skrev, \"Spelet fick lära mig att Baker av sin far, som i sin tur lärt sig det från en engelsman under 1920-talet.\" Denna variant kallas nu Bakers spel. För att utföra en intressant komplexitet analys måste man konstruera en generaliserad version av Kungen spel med 4 * n kort. The deck consists of 108 cards, of which there are 25 of each color (red, green, blue, and yellow), each color having two of each rank except zero. The ranks in each color are zero to nine, \"Skip\", \"Draw Two\", and \"Reverse\" (the last three being \"action cards\"). In addition, the deck contains four each of \"Wild\" and \"Wild Draw Four\" cards\r\n\r\nEach player is dealt 7 cards and the remaining cards are placed face down to form a draw pile. The first player has to match the card in the discard pile either by number or color or the player can throw down a Wild Card else he must pick a card from the draw pile. If he can play what is drawn, great.
